 When he was asked how the Gods and Goddesses cannot think and think like ordinary people, how will they transfer property, then Sinir Advocate Jitendra Mohan Sharma said that the way a company is a legal person and its director or trustee The Hindu deities also exercise their legal rights through their representatives
 unhone bataaya ki hinduon ke devi-devtaa bhi company yaa naaballig kii tarah sampatti arjeet karte hai or pratinidhi ke jariye court main cese ladate hai

 iskaa matlab yah he ki natural person ko samvidhan main die gaye moulik adhikaar or kanoonee adhikaar donon die jate hai, jabaki juristic person yani legal intity ko sirfkanoonee adhikarhi die jate hai
 Since when did Hindu deities get legal rights in India? Hindu deities in India were first considered a juristic person in the British era in 1888
 hindu devi-devataaon ko skool, college chalaane or trust banane kaa bhi kanoonee adhikaar mila he
 The court has already considered Hindu deities as legal persons in dozens of cases including Manohar Ganesh Tambekar vs
 Lakhmiram Govindram, Bhupathi Nath Smritithirtha vs
 Ram Lal Maitra, Rampat vs
 Durga Bharati, Ram Brahma vs
 Kedarnath

 ) (except for the headline, this news has not been edited by the NDTV team, it is published directly from the Syndicate feed
 ) Every person wants to make their home beautiful and live in peace
 lekin shaharon kii badhati aabaadi or rahane laayak jameen kii kami ke kaaran vaastushastra ke anusaar manachaahi bhoomikhand milanaa mushkil-sa ho gaya he
 In such a situation, people are forced to take plots or flats given by urban development authorities or private builders
 lekin praaia: ye plot yaa flats puri tarah se vaastu ke anusaar nahin hote hai
 There are many types of Vaastu defects in such plots or flats, which cause many problems in life
 - bhartiya vaastushastra ke anusaar in vaastudosha ko dur yaa kam karne ke liye ghar kii aantarik sajja vishesh madadgaar hoti hai
 Undoubtedly the color and curtains of the walls play an important role in the interior decoration of the house
 - isliye ghar kii deevaaron or pardon ke rang kaa sahi chunaav karnaa chahie taaki sakaaratmak urja or samruddhi main vruddhi ho
 Different colored curtains not only make the house beautiful, but also helps in maintaining positive energy in the house
 - chunki ghar ke har kamare kaa uddeshy alag-alag hota he
 Indian Vastu Shastra should not paint all rooms in the house with the same color
 - maansik shanti or rishton main madhurata ke liye rang kaa vaigyanik mahatv he
 Putting the bedrooms in pink, sky or light green color increases the positive energy
 - kichan ke liye laal or naarangi shubh rang mana jaataa he
 White or light blue color is suitable for toilet and bathroom
 - ghar main pardaa lagaana ho yah dhyaan rakhen ki parde hameshaa do rang kii paraton vaali honi chahie
 If the bedroom is in the east direction, green curtains are good
 - uttar disha ke kamare liye nile parde or pashchim disha ke kamare ke liye safed rang ke parde lagaana uchit mana gaya he
 If the room is at the corner of south direction then red colored curtains are considered suitable
 - drawing room yani baithak ghar kaa kaaphi mahatvapurn cameraa hota he
 The walls of this room are considered to be light blue or sky, cream color, yellow or light green
 is kamare liye kriim, safed, sunahare yaa bhure rang kaa pardon prayog kiya ja saktaa he
 - Light green, light gray, white or cream color should be used in the drawing room made in the aerial direction
 yadi drawing room kii khidkiyaan-daravaaje main uttar disha main hon to hare aadhaar par nile rang se bani jal kii laharon jaisi dizin ke parde uttam hote hai
 According to Indian architecture, the sealing of the house plays the role of Brahmasthan and this brings positive energy to the house
 yadi aap apane ghar kii ceiling ko gulabi, pile, nile aadi rangon se putavana chaahate hai to rukiye kyonki chhaton kaa rang safed hi sarvottam mana gaya he
 The comments - yadi ghar main puja ghar banwaaya he to is deevaaron ko halkaa nila rang se rangavaana chahie kyonki yah viratata, shanti or ekaagratha kaa pratik he
 - There should not be a place of worship in the bedroom, but if there is a compulsion to make a place of worship in the bedroom, then the arrangement of curtains is very important
 iske liye safed, halke pilaa, halke gulabi yaa sunahare rang ke parde shubh maane gaye hai
 According to Indian Vastu Shastra, interior decoration of the house is especially helpful to remove or reduce these Vastu defects
 nihsandeh ghar ke interior decoration main deevaaron ke rang or pardon kii mahatvapurn bhoomika he
 Therefore, the color of the walls and curtains of the house should be chosen properly so that positive energy and prosperity can increase
 alag-alag rang ke parde ghar ko na keval khubasurat banaate hai, balki ghar main positive energy banaae rakhane main sahaayak hote hai
 - Since the purpose of each room of the house is different
 bhartiya vaastushastra ghar ke sabhi kamaron kii putai ek hi rang se nahin karwaani chahie
 - Color has scientific significance for mental peace and sweetness in relationships
 bedrum ko gulabi, aasamaani yaa halke hare rang se putai karwaane se sakaaratmak urja main vruddhi hoti he
 - Red and orange are considered auspicious colors for the kitchen
 toilet or bathrum ke liye safed yaa halkaa nila rang anukool hota he
 - To cover the curtain in the house, keep in mind that the curtains should always be of two color layers
 yadi bedrum purv disha main ho to hare rang ke parde achche hote hai
 - Blue curtains for rooms in north direction and white curtains for rooms in west direction is considered appropriate
 yadi cameraa dakshin disha ke kone par ho to laal rang ke parde upyukt maane gaye hai
 - The drawing room is a very important room in the living room
 is kamare kii deevaaron ko halke nile yaa aasamaani, kriim color, pilaa yaa halke hare rang kaa hona uttam mana gaya he
 Cream, white, golden or brown curtains can be used for this room
 - vivy disha main bane drawing room main halkaa haraa, halakaa slate, safed yaa kriim rang kaa prayog kiya janaa chahie
 If the windows and doors of the drawing room are in the north direction, then curtains designed like blue water waves on a green base are perfect
 - bhartiya vaastushastra ke anusaar ghar kii ceiling brahmasthaan kii bhoomika nibhaati he or isse ghar main positive energy aati he
 If you want to paint the ceiling of your house with pink, yellow, blue, etc
 then stop because white is considered the best color of roofs
 tippaniyan - If a house of worship is built in the house, then these walls should be painted in light blue color because it is a symbol of greatness, peace and concentration
 - shayan kaksh main puujagrih nahin hona chahie, lekin shayankaksh main puja-sthaan bananaa majaburi ho to vahaan parde kii vyavastha bahut jaruri he
